of Arab States: its attempt to settle the dispute took the form of a neutral resolution without any call for action.</span></p></td><td class="cl-93432b36"><p class="cl-9342efae"><span two countries, withdrew its ambassador from Phnom Penh, and suspended air service between the capitals.</span></p></td><td class="cl-93585baa"><p class="cl-935835b2"><span determination to rearm Germany, Khrushchev decided upon harsher measures.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9361889d"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">No</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144ea">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9361889c"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">168.13</span></p></td><td class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">In a speech on 10 November 1958 he announced that the Soviet Union intended to turn over control of East Berlin, including all access routes to West Berlin, to East Germany, thus forcing the West to recognize and to deal with East Germany.</span></p></td><td class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">High tension, normal in the Cold War, was approaching crisis intensity.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9361889d"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">No</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144ea">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9361889c"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">168.15</span></p></td><td class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">Khrushchev, increasingly concerned about publicly announced U.S.-NATO plans to nuclearize the East/West conflict in Europe, especially the West German army, and to undermine the DDR, and under mounting pressure from East Germany's Walter Ulbricht, initiated a crisis for France, the U.K., the U.S., and West Germany by an ultimatum on 27 November 1958.</span></p></td><td class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">NA</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144fe">crisis</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144ea">about</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144fe">13</span><span class="cl-936144ea">A Note to the four Western ambassadors in Moscow proposed that West Berlin be demilitarized and declared a "Free City," a status that would be guaranteed by the Western powers, the Soviet Union, and, perhaps, the United Nations.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9361889d"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">No</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144ea">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9361889c"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">168.17</span></p></td><td class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">If no agreement could be reached on this proposal within six months, the Soviet government would turn over to the DDR full sovereignty over East Berlin, including access routes to West Berlin.</span></p></td><td class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">NA</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144ea">No</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> </span><span class="cl-936144ea">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-936188a6"><p that the six months constituted an ultimatum but stated that Moscow did indeed intend to carry out its proposals; and should the West use force against the Ulbricht regime, the USSR was committed militarily to the defense of East Germany as a Warsaw Pact ally.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9361889d"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">NA</span><span class="cl-936144ea"> class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144ea">On 11 December the Tass news agency warned that a Western attempt to force its way into West Berlin by land, an option considered in the 1948 Berlin Blockade crisis, would lead to war.</span></p></td><td class="cl-93618892"><p class="cl-93615048"><span class="cl-936144fe">Soviet</span><span class="cl-936144fe"> </span><span class="cl-936a5c56">Mexican fishers had been fishing for shrimp in what Guatemala considered its territorial waters.</span></p></td><td class="cl-936a937e"><p class="cl-936a6ba6"><span his perception of a crisis stemming from an economic threat from Mexico and warned it of impending attack if its fishers did not leave Guatemalan waters.</span></p></td><td class="cl-936a9393"><p class="cl-936a6ba6"><span class="cl-936a5c60">Guatemala</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span class="cl-936a5c56">initiated</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span </span><span class="cl-936a5c56">following</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span class="cl-936a5c56">will</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span class="cl-936a5c60">happen</span><span </span><span class="cl-936a5c56">NA</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-936a9388"><p class="cl-936a6ba6"><span class="cl-936a5c56">169.5</span></p></td><td off the Pacific coast, killing three fishers and wounding 14 others.</span></p></td><td class="cl-936a937e"><p class="cl-936a6ba6"><span class="cl-936a5c60">Guatemala</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span class="cl-936a5c56">initiated</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span class="cl-936a5c60">attack</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span class="cl-936a5c56">toward</span><span January 1959.</span></p></td><td class="cl-936a9393"><p class="cl-936a6ba6"><span class="cl-936a5c56">No</span><span class="cl-936a5c56"> </span><span
